name:V‚Äçi‚Äçv‚Äçi‚ÄçL‚Äçe‚Äço‚Äçn
info:Elegant Room - Garden-View
info:Stayed in December 2023
info:Friends
info:43 Reviews
rating:4.2
posted:Posted January 8, 2024
msg:I recently stayed at Resort Golden Palm in Sanya and my experience was a mix of highs and lows. The initial encounter with the lobby staff wasn't very pleasant, but the rest of the staff throughout my stay were exceptionally friendly. The hotel's prime location, just across the beach and 800 meters from restaurants, malls, and markets, adds significant value.

The highlight of the resort is undoubtedly its amazing pool and lake. Additionally, the unexpected gifts of a complimentary photoshoot and fishing experience were a pleasant surprise. The photoshoot was entirely free, allowing me to choose five pictures with the option to purchase extras at a reasonable price.

I opted for the fishing experience, but since I wasn't familiar with it, the staff kindly replaced it with a fish foot spa, showcasing their flexibility and commitment to guest satisfaction.

On the downside, I booked the cheapest room, which proved to be spacious but disappointing. The room had an old and unpleasant smell, and the bathroom felt like it belonged to a 2-star hotel with its outdated and dark features. This aspect significantly affected my overall impression.

Despite this, the hotel's proximity to the area's best hotels and the positive encounters with most staff members leave me considering a future stay, with the hope of exploring a different room for a potentially improved experience. Addressing the room conditions could significantly enhance the overall appeal of Resort Golden Palm.
----------------------------------------

name:Y‚Äça‚ÄçL‚Äçe‚Äçn‚Äçk‚Äça
info:Cozy Room - Garden-View
info:Stayed in July 2022
info:Couples
info:6 Reviews
rating:4.2
posted:Posted July 30, 2022
msg:Hi everyone! The hotel is a little bit old, but it's nice, clean and the staff is very friendly, although almost everybody didn't speak English. 
- The breakfast was quite appropriate for a foreigner: fried eggs, french fries, cereal, coffee from a coffee machine, some fried chicken with vegetables, some kinds of steamed and baked buns, watermelon and melon, cherry tomatoes and lettuce with some salad dressings. 
- The room is clean, the hotel provides shampoo, shower gel, and lotion, a hairdryer, two cups, two glasses, some teabags, bottled water, and fresh towels every day. There were two bathrobes and towels for the beach with a bag where you can put your towel. We have been living in three different rooms because at first, we came for 2 days and lived in a comfortable room with a garden view 2408 on the 4th floor, it was the best room. Then we decided to move to dadonghai and after 3 days we came back to this hotel again and lived in a room with a swimming pool and a lake view 2603 on the 6th floor for 4 more days. On the last evening, two small lizards appeared in the room and we asked the staff to change the room for 1 night, they were very nice and they agreed and gave us room 1107 on the first floor with a swimming pool view, the room was for a family with a child and had some toys inside. The first two rooms had a bathtub, the third one had a shower. All three rooms were with a balcony. 
- The swimming pool area is awesome, very beautiful, and clean. The deck chairs were very cozy, the swimming pool was quite clean. There are some hammocks and a swing with a lake view where you can enjoy the quietness and have a rest.
- The beachside is near, just across the road, the beach is clean, the sand is white and beautiful, and the sea is quite clean, there were some deck chairs and sunshades. You can have fun with some water activities at the beach too if you want of course. 
There are not so many cafes and restaurants appropriate for foreign people except Subway, McDonald's, Starbucks, KFC, and Pizza Hut. If there were a little bit more western food cafes close to the beachside, I would definitely recommend this place to everyone.
If you want to have a lazy and quiet holiday you should go there and relax!

This depth is impossible for people who can swim, and it is late in the off-season. It was closed at 7 o'clock and no swimming was allowed, leaving only a few shallow water children's pools. I hope the merchant can write clearly that the depth of deep water is actually about 1.3 meters, and an adult who can't swim at about 1.7 meters will not feel pressured. As for going to the public beach to swim, the waves are very big, and the mouth and eyes are full of salt when the waves come down, even those who can swim will not be able to swim. If you want to swim, it is recommended to rent a swimming ring. The hotel needs to cross a road from the public beach. There are no traffic lights in Sanya, and the road is narrow, so be careful when crossing the road. You can swim on the public beach, but there are many people. If you stay at the private beach of a hotel in Haitang Bay, it is generally guarded and you cannot swim. There is a gym in the hotel that is not big and almost no one goes there. There is a suspension bridge behind the swimming pool garden. There is a forest across the suspension bridge, and there is a sign beside it. There are insects such as snakes and thunder horses in the forest. None of this is a big deal, I just wonder how did a spider the size of a walnut get in on the floor of my room on the third night? The doors and windows are all closed, so it must not be a day or two in the room, right? Did he come in while cleaning the room? If you want to change to another girl, you will be too scared to sleep. (The spider is poisonous and I stomped it flat.) I advise everyone not to live on the first floor. There is a bus stop at the entrance of the hotel but there is no stop sign. Friends who want to take the bus should pay attention. Turn right at the exit and walk for about 15 minutes to the Baihuagu Commercial Street, where there are all kinds of food, drink and entertainment. There is nothing to see in the central square of Yalong Bay, just a sculpture. 20 minutes is enough to take a photo in a circle. It only takes about 20 minutes to take a taxi to the Tropical Rainforest Forest Park, and it takes about 25 minutes to walk to Yalong Bay Underwater World. In short, the overall value of this hotel is not bad, and it has everything you need. But friends who want to pursue higher quality and not bad money suggest choosing Haitang Bay.
